state is structured and normalized.\\\\n\\\\n## Goals\\\\n\\\\n### Primary goals\\\\n\\\\n- Reduce hallucination in long-form and multi-step output.\\\\n- Reduce drift from initial task, definitions, and constraints.\\\\n- Establish durable continuity through self-tags and pointer chains.\\\\n- Ground factual and computational claims in retrieval or deterministic tools.\\\\n- Build reflective memory as a first-class system component.\\\\n- Introduce valence-like adaptation from interaction outcomes.\\\\n- Create a foundation for structured self-model alignment.\\\\n- Enable optional inter-agent comparison of local meaning and valence models.\\\\n\\\\n### Secondary goals\\\\n\\\\n- Improve user trust through evidence and explicit uncertainty.\\\\n- Provide a serious technical substrate for research into emergence-like machine behavior.\\\\n- Make state and reasoning inspectable for operators and developers.\\\\n- Support local-first or hybrid deployment modes appropriate for privacy-sensitive projects.\\\\n\\\\n### Non-goals\\\\n\\\\n- Proving true consciousness.\\\\n- Declaring that a continuity-rich agent is sentient.\\\\n- Reproducing full biological brain function.\\\\n- Replacing human philosophical judgment with system metrics.\\\\n- Treating operational valence as equivalent to phenomenal feeling.\\\\n\\\\n## System Scope\\\\n\\\\n### In scope\\\\n\\\\n- Persistent state and continuity management\\\\n- Goal contracts and structured planning\\\\n- Claim budgeting and claim verification\\\\n- Retrieval and memory integration\\\\n- Deterministic compute integration\\\\n- Generator/verifier separation\\\\n- Repair/replan control loops\\\\n- Reflective archiving\\\\n- Valence learning from interaction outcomes\\\\n- Self-tag and pointer-chain maintenance\\\\n- Optional inter-agent comparison layer\\\\n- Observability, runbooks, and failure recovery\\\\n\\\\n### Out of scope\\\\n\\\\n- Strong sentience claims\\\\n- Complete biological emulation\\\\n- Universal emotion theory\\\\n- Fully unconstrained autonomous action\\\\n- Any claim that continuity alone proves subjective experience\\\\n\\\\n### Assumptions\\\\n\\\\n- The system has access to durable storage.\\\\n- Tooling can be integrated into an orchestrated workflow.\\\\n- The base model supports structured prompting or programmatic control.\\\\n- Users and operators can provide at least some explicit or implicit feedback signals.\\\\n- The system can legally and ethically retain approved interaction-derived state.\\\\n\\\\n### Constraints\\\\n\\\\n- Context window limitations remain binding.\\\\n- Tool latency may be non-trivial.\\\\n- Deterministic compute tooling may require licensing and local installation.\\\\n- Privacy and consent boundaries restrict what can be stored or shared.\\\\n- Richer statefulness increases operational complexity.\\\\n\\\\n## Requirements\\\\n\\\\n### Functional requirements\\\\n\\\\nFR-1: The system shall create a Goal Contract for every non-trivial task.\\\\nFR-2: The system shall create a Plan Skeleton before final language generation.\\\\nFR-3: The system shall create and track a Claim Budget for any claim-bearing output.\\\\nFR-4: The system shall retrieve or compute support for non-trivial factual claims where feasible.\\\\nFR-5: The system shall label unsupported material as inferred, hypothetical, or unknown.\\\\nFR-6: The system shall separate generation from verification.\\\\nFR-7: The system shall prevent finalization of output when verifier checks fail above threshold.\\\\nFR-8: The system shall maintain a persistent Experience Archive.\\\\nFR-9: The system shall write Self-tags at configured continuity boundaries.\\\\nFR-10: The system shall maintain Pointer Chains linking self-tags over time.\\\\nFR-11: The system shall derive Valence Signals from interaction outcomes.\\\\nFR-12: The system shall update Valence Maps using weighted and auditable logic.\\\\nFR-13: The system shall support deterministic compute integration for structured tasks.\\\\nFR-14: The system shall expose metrics and logs for drift, hallucination proxies, retrieval quality, and chain\\\\nintegrity.\\\\nFR-15: The system shall support optional normalized inter-agent comparison workflows.\\\\n\\\\n### Non-functional requirements\\\\n\\\\n- Traceability: every material claim must map to evidence, computation, or explicit inference.\\\\n- Interpretability: core state objects must be inspectable.\\\\n- Extensibility: modules must be replaceable without redesigning the whole stack.\\\\n- Recoverability: state corruption must be detectable and repairable.\\\\n- Latency discipline: workflows must permit adaptive depth based on task risk.\\\\n\\\\n### Operational requirements\\\\n\\\\n- Scheduled archive compaction\\\\n- Scheduled pointer-chain integrity checks\\\\n- Health checks for compute and retrieval backends\\\\n- Runbooks for verifier failure storms and memory corruption events\\\\n- Support for policy-based deletion and redaction\\\\n\\\\n### Security and privacy requirements\\\\n\\\\n- Encryption at rest and in transit\\\\n- Fine-grained authorization for memory partitions and tools\\\\n- Retention controls honoring consent and minimization\\\\n- Sanitized compute and CLI execution paths\\\\n- Privacy-preserving inter-agent comparison outputs\\\\n\\\\n### Reliability requirements\\\\n\\\\n- Safe degradation when retrieval or compute backends fail\\\\n- Explicit uncertainty instead of unsupported completion\\\\n- Retry logic with bounded loops\\\\n- Versioned state and rollback support\\\\n\\\\n### Scalability requirements\\\\n\\\\n- Support many task runs over long time horizons\\\\n- Support growth of archives and indexes without collapse in retrieval quality\\\\n- Support optional multi-agent population-level comparison jobs\\\\n\\\\n## Architecture Overview\\\\n\\\\n### High-level architecture\\\\n\\\\n```text\\\\n+--------------------+\\\\n| Human / Operator |\\\\n+---------+----------+\\\\n|\\\\nv\\\\n+-----------------------------+\\\\n| Input / Perception Layer |\\\\n| prompts, events, telemetry |\\\\n+-------------+---------------+\\\\n|\\\\nv\\\\n+-----------------------------+\\\\n| Goal Contract Builder\\\\n|\\\\n+-------------+---------------+\\\\n|\\\\nv\\\\n+-----------------------------+\\\\n| Planning / Structuring |\\\\n| Plan Skeleton + ClaimBudget |\\\\n+-------------+---------------+\\\\n|\\\\n+-------+--------+\\\\n|\\\\n|\\\\nv\\\\nv\\\\n+-------------+ +-------------------+\\\\n| Retrieval / | | Deterministic |\\\\n| Memory | | Compute Adapter |\\\\n+------+------+ +---------+---------+\\\\n|\\\\n|\\\\n+----------+---------+\\\\n|\\\\nv\\\\n+-----------------------------+\\\\n| Generator\\\\n|\\\\n| constrained narrative\\\\n|\\\\n+-------------+---------------+\\\\n|\\\\nv\\\\n+-----------------------------+\\\\n| Verifier / Critic\\\\n|\\\\n| grounding, drift, support |\\\\n+-------------+---------------+\\\\nfail / \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\ pass\\\\n/ \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\nv v\\\\n+-----------------------------+ +----------------------+\\\\n| Repair / Re-plan\\\\n| | Final Output\\\\n|\\\\n+-------------+---------------+\\\\n+----------+-----------+\\\\n|\\\\n|\\\\nv\\\\nv\\\\n+-----------------------------+ +----------------------+\\\\n| Reflection / Archive\\\\n|<-----| Outcome / Feedback |\\\\n| self-tags, valence, logs | | engagement, edits |\\\\n+-------------+---------------+\\\\n+----------+-----------+\\\\n|\\\\nv\\\\n+-----------------------------+\\\\n| Inter-Agent Comparison |\\\\n| optional consensus layer |\\\\n+-----------------------------+\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n### Main components\\\\n\\\\n- Input / Perception Layer\\\\n- Goal Contract Builder\\\\n- Planning / Structuring Engine\\\\n- Retrieval and Memory Layer\\\\n- Deterministic Compute Adapter\\\\n- Generator\\\\n- Verifier / Critic\\\\n- Repair / Re-plan Controller\\\\n- Reflection / Experience Archive\\\\n- Valence Learning Module\\\\n- Self-Tag and Pointer Chain Store\\\\n- Inter-Agent Comparison Layer\\\\n- Observability and Operations Layer\\\\n\\\\n### Data flow summary\\\\n\\\\n- User or system input enters through the perception layer.\\\\n- A Goal Contract anchors the run.\\\\n- A Plan Skeleton and Claim Budget externalize intended structure.\\\\n- Retrieval and computation gather support.\\\\n- The Generator renders a draft.\\\\n- The Verifier approves, blocks, or requests repair.\\\\n- Final outputs and outcomes are archived.\\\\n- Reflection writes self-tags, updates continuity, and applies valence updates.\\\\n- Optional inter-agent services compare local learned structures.\\\\n\\\\n### External integrations\\\\n\\\\n- Retrieval/indexing systems\\\\n- Deterministic compute backend such as Wolfram Engine invoked through WolframScript\\\\n- Databases and object storage\\\\n- Scheduler / queue systems\\\\n- Optional local-first file or vector storage systems\\\\n\\\\n### Human-in-the-loop touchpoints\\\\n\\\\n- Task initiation\\\\n- Corrections\\\\n- Explicit ratings\\\\n- Review of blocked outputs\\\\n- Approval gates for sensitive actions\\\\n- Interpretation of research results involving self-modeling\\\\n\\\\n## Detailed Component Design\\\\n\\\\n### Input / Perception Layer\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nNormalize prompts, interaction outcomes, telemetry, and tool results into canonical ingest objects.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- Capture all inbound task-bearing input\\\\n- Capture engagement and correction events\\\\n- Timestamp and source-tag all events\\\\n- Route task vs feedback vs telemetry events\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- User prompts\\\\n- Event notifications\\\\n- Tool outputs\\\\n- Session metadata\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\nInputEnvelope\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- Event typing\\\\n- Metadata normalization\\\\n- Security classification\\\\n- Provenance assignment\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- API/UI entry points\\\\n- tool adapters\\\\n- event bus\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- malformed payloads\\\\n- missing provenance\\\\n- duplicated events\\\\n- incorrect classification\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- ingest throughput\\\\n- schema validation failures\\\\n- event latency\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- sanitize payloads\\\\n- preserve auth context\\\\n- strip prohibited fields before downstream routing\\\\n\\\\n### Goal Contract Builder\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nCreate the canonical anti-drift anchor for a task.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- Extract task objective\\\\n- Extract constraints\\\\n- Define success criteria\\\\n- Mark assumptions and unknowns\\\\n- Label inferred structure as inferred\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\nInputEnvelope\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\nGoalContract\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- Parse explicit request\\\\n- Resolve implicit structure only when necessary\\\\n- Freeze the active scope for this run\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- state store\\\\n- instruction templates or parser logic\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- hidden scope expansion\\\\n- incorrect assumptions\\\\n- insufficiently explicit success criteria\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- goal/final divergence score\\\\n- assumption count\\\\n- inferred material count\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- Do not infer or attach unauthorized external context\\\\n\\\\n### Planning / Structuring Engine\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nExternalize latent intent into explicit intermediate structures before language generation.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- Create Plan Skeleton\\\\n- Create Claim Budget\\\\n- Create entity and dependency maps\\\\n- Surface unknowns and evidence requirements\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- GoalContract\\\\n- relevant memory/evidence stubs\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\n- PlanSkeleton\\\\n- ClaimBudget\\\\n- EntityMap\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- decompose goal into sections and dependencies\\\\n- identify claims requiring support\\\\n- sequence\\\\n\\\\nnecessary retrieval or compute steps\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- state store\\\\n- retrieval hints\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- omitted dependencies\\\\n- plan too vague to constrain generation\\\\n- premature narrative creep\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- plan completeness metrics\\\\n- unsupported-claim forecast count\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- Internal-only structures must not leak unless intentionally exposed\\\\n\\\\n### Retrieval and Memory Layer\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nProvide relevant evidence and continuity state for current reasoning.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- retrieve episodic and semantic memory\\\\n- retrieve external documents and structured facts\\\\n- attach provenance and freshness metadata\\\\n- support relevance ranking and reranking\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- queries from planner and verifier\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\n- EvidenceBundle\\\\n- MemoryBundle\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- query rewriting\\\\n- retrieval across stores\\\\n- provenance preservation\\\\n- freshness-aware ranking\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- document store\\\\n- relational/state DB\\\\n- optional vector index\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- stale hits\\\\n- irrelevant hits\\\\n- low recall\\\\n- provenance loss\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- hit rate\\\\n- relevance quality\\\\n- freshness distribution\\\\n- citation coverage\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- per-source authorization\\\\n- redaction where necessary\\\\n- scope-limited retrieval\\\\n\\\\n### Deterministic Compute Adapter\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nRoute symbolic, numeric, or formally computable tasks to deterministic backends.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- convert structured task fragments into compute commands\\\\n- invoke local compute engine\\\\n- parse and validate results\\\\n- preserve compute provenance\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- structured compute requests from planner, generator, or verifier\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\n- ComputeInvocationRecord\\\\n- machine-readable compute results\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- task-to-command translation\\\\n- execute via WolframScript or equivalent\\\\n- parse output into canonical schema\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- Wolfram Engine / WolframScript or other deterministic runtime\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- CLI execution failure\\\\n- malformed output\\\\n- tool not installed or not activated\\\\n- licensing constraints\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- execution latency\\\\n- failure rate\\\\n- parse failure rate\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- sanitize commands\\\\n- sandbox execution\\\\n- do not expose secrets in logs\\\\n\\\\n### Generator\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nRender structured state into final language or action instructions without exceeding evidence bounds.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- generate draft text/artifacts\\\\n- preserve section structure\\\\n- maintain support-class labeling where\\\\n\\\\nneeded\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- Goal Contract\\\\n- Plan Skeleton\\\\n- Claim Budget\\\\n- evidence and compute results\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\ndraft output\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- map structure to prose\\\\n- insert caveats where support is incomplete\\\\n- avoid unsupported\\\\n\\\\nelaboration\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- planner\\\\n- retrieval and compute outputs\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- embellishment\\\\n- local coherence over truth\\\\n- omission of uncertainty markers\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- support coverage ratio\\\\n- prose length vs evidence density\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- redact restricted content\\\\n- maintain provenance boundaries\\\\n\\\\n### Verifier / Critic\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nIndependently assess whether a draft is accurate, supported, in-scope, and structurally aligned.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- verify support for claims\\\\n- verify consistency with Goal Contract\\\\n- detect drift and contradiction\\\\n\\\\n- classify unsupported or speculative material - enforce finalization threshold\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- draft\\\\n- Goal Contract\\\\n- Claim Budget\\\\n- evidence and compute outputs\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\nVerificationReport\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- claim-to-support mapping\\\\n- drift scoring\\\\n- contradiction and omission detection\\\\n- severity\\\\n\\\\nassignment\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- retrieval and compute\\\\n- policy/rules layer\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- false negatives on unsupported claims\\\\n- false positives blocking acceptable output\\\\n- validator\\\\n\\\\ncollapse if insufficiently independent from generator logic\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- pass/fail ratio\\\\n- issue type distribution\\\\n- mean repair count\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\nverifier gets least-privilege access to necessary state and evidence only\\\\n\\\\n### Repair / Re-plan Controller\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nAttempt targeted recovery after verification failure without widening scope recklessly.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- invoke targeted retrieval\\\\n- revise claims or plan\\\\n- constrain regeneration\\\\n- escalate to explicit\\\\n\\\\nuncertainty when necessary\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\nVerificationReport\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\nrepaired plan/draft or structured defer/unknown result\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- classify issue type\\\\n- select retrieval vs replan vs defer\\\\n- prevent infinite loops with bounded retry\\\\n\\\\nlimits\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- planner\\\\n- retriever\\\\n- generator\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- repeated repair loops\\\\n- over-pruning nuance\\\\n- accidental scope broadening\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- retry counts\\\\n- repair success rate\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\nno broadening of source access without authorization\\\\n\\\\n### Reflection / Experience Archive\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nPersist what happened so that continuity and adaptation can exist beyond the immediate run.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- log outcomes, feedback, corrections, verifier reports, and summaries\\\\n- generate state deltas write self-tags\\\\n- support future retrieval and compaction\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- final outputs\\\\n- interaction outcomes\\\\n- verification data\\\\n- task metadata\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\n- versioned archive records\\\\n- reflection summaries\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- summarize task outcome\\\\n- identify what changed\\\\n- preserve provenance links\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- durable storage\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- archive corruption\\\\n- noisy or redundant accumulation\\\\n- unbounded growth\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- write success/failure\\\\n- archive growth curves\\\\n- compaction efficiency\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- encryption\\\\n- retention controls\\\\n- redaction-aware storage policy\\\\n\\\\n### Valence Learning Module\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nTranslate interaction outcomes into directional operational weighting without claiming phenomenology.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- detect positive/negative/neutral interaction outcomes\\\\n- compute weighted updates\\\\n- separate user-local and broader trends\\\\n- decay stale or low-confidence signals\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- engagement duration\\\\n- abandonment\\\\n- explicit ratings\\\\n- corrections\\\\n- repeated satisfaction or dissatisfaction patterns\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\n- updated ValenceMap\\\\n- auditable ValenceSignal records\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- weighted update rules\\\\n- anomaly filtering\\\\n- confidence and scope assignment\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- archive\\\\n- analytics pipeline\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- reward hacking\\\\n- poisoning by adversarial or noisy feedback\\\\n- overgeneralizing one user’s preferences globally\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- valence shift trends\\\\n- signal confidence distribution\\\\n- poisoning anomaly alerts\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- minimize retention of raw sensitive interaction data\\\\n- preserve audit trails for updates\\\\n\\\\n### Self-Tag and Pointer Chain Store\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nProvide a formal continuity substrate modeled as linked state checkpoints.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- write self-tags at meaningful boundaries\\\\n- link current self-tag to predecessor\\\\n- support\\\\n\\\\nrecursive continuity tracing and summarization\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- reflection summaries\\\\n- state snapshots\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\n- SelfTag\\\\n- pointer links\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- version state\\\\n- compute signatures or hashes\\\\n- maintain branch-aware chain integrity\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\nstate/metadata store\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- broken pointers\\\\n- duplicate tags\\\\n- ambiguous branching semantics\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- continuity integrity score\\\\n- branch frequency\\\\n- broken-link count\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\nstate snapshots may include sensitive information and must be tightly controlled\\\\n\\\\n### Inter-Agent Comparison Layer\\\\n\\\\n**Purpose**\\\\n\\\\nCompare local meaning and valence structures across multiple agents in a normalized and privacy-preserving\\\\nway.\\\\n\\\\n**Responsibilities**\\\\n- collect normalized summaries\\\\n- compute convergence and divergence\\\\n- identify stable shared\\\\n\\\\nstructures vs local idiosyncrasies\\\\n\\\\n**Inputs**\\\\n- agent-local valence maps\\\\n- scenario judgments\\\\n- structured self-description summaries\\\\n\\\\n**Outputs**\\\\n- consensus/divergence reports\\\\n- comparison records\\\\n\\\\n**Internal logic**\\\\n- normalize schema\\\\n- compute overlap and divergence metrics\\\\n- preserve plurality rather than forcing collapse\\\\n\\\\n**Dependencies**\\\\n- multiple participating agent instances\\\\n- shared protocol definitions\\\\n\\\\n**Failure modes**\\\\n- false consensus\\\\n- collapse of diversity\\\\n- privacy leakage through over-detailed summaries\\\\n\\\\n**Observability**\\\\n- convergence stability\\\\n- divergence clustering\\\\n- comparison freshness\\\\n\\\\n**Security**\\\\n- prefer abstract summaries and aggregates over raw logs\\\\n- preserve user privacy across agent boundaries\\\\n\\\\n## Data Model and Information Design\\\\n\\\\n### Core entities\\\\n\\\\n- InputEnvelope\\\\n- GoalContract\\\\n- PlanSkeleton\\\\n- ClaimBudget\\\\n- EvidenceBundle\\\\n- VerificationReport\\\\n- ExperienceRecord\\\\n- ValenceSignal\\\\n- ValenceMap\\\\n- SelfTag\\\\n- PointerLink\\\\n- AgentComparisonRecord\\\\n- ComputeInvocationRecord\\\\n\\\\n### Example schemas\\\\n\\\\n#### GoalContract\\\\n\\\\n```json\\\\n{\\\\n\\\\\\\"goal_id\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"gc_2026_03_10_001\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"task\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"Produce grounded technical specification and white paper\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"success_criteria\\\\\\\": [\\\\n\\\\\\\"Exhaustive structure\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"All inferred material labeled\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"Open conflicts captured\\\\\\\"\\\\n],\\\\n\\\\\\\"constraints\\\\\\\": [\\\\n\\\\\\\"Use polished Markdown\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"Preserve coined terminology\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"Avoid loose summarization\\\\\\\"\\\\n],\\\\n\\\\\\\"assumptions\\\\\\\": [\\\\n\\\\\\\"Current design corpus is authoritative source material\\\\\\\"\\\\n],\\\\n\\\\\\\"unknowns\\\\\\\": [],\\\\n\\\\\\\"inferred_from_design_corpus\\\\\\\": [\\\\n\\\\\\\"Formal architecture names required for implementation clarity\\\\\\\"\\\\n],\\\\n\\\\\\\"created_at\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"2026-03-10T00:00:00Z\\\\\\\"\\\\n}\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n#### ClaimBudget\\\\n\\\\n```json\\\\n{\\\\n\\\\\\\"claims\\\\\\\": [\\\\n{\\\\n\\\\\\\"claim_id\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"cl_001\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"text\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"Hallucination and drift can be modeled as serialization and state-management failures.\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"type\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"design_corpus_architectural_inference\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"support_required\\\\\\\": true,\\\\n\\\\\\\"support_sources\\\\\\\": [\\\\\\\"design_corpus\\\\\\\"],\\\\n\\\\\\\"status\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"supported_by_design_corpus_inference\\\\\\\"\\\\n}\\\\n]\\\\n}\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n#### SelfTag\\\\n\\\\n```json\\\\n{\\\\n\\\\\\\"self_tag_id\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"st_2026_03_10_145500\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"previous_self_tag_id\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"st_2026_03_09_231000\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"state_signature\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"sha256:...\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"summary\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"Completed verifier-gated output loop and updated valence map after reflected correction.\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"goals_active\\\\\\\": [\\\\\\\"reduce drift\\\\\\\", \\\\\\\"preserve continuity\\\\\\\"],\\\\n\\\\\\\"valence_snapshot_ref\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"vm_8821\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"created_at\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"2026-03-10T14:55:00Z\\\\\\\"\\\\n}\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n#### ValenceSignal\\\\n\\\\n```json\\\\n{\\\\n\\\\\\\"signal_id\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"vs_4471\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"context\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"User disengaged after unsupported verbose explanation\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"event_type\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"engagement_drop\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"direction\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"negative\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"magnitude\\\\\\\": 0.42,\\\\n\\\\\\\"scope\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"user_specific\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"source\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"interaction_outcome\\\\\\\",\\\\n\\\\\\\"created_at\\\\\\\": \\\\\\\"2026-03-10T15:02:00Z\\\\\\\"\\\\n}\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n### Relationships\\\\n\\\\n- One GoalContract owns many claim records.\\\\n- One ExperienceRecord can generate one or more ValenceSignal records.\\\\n- One ExperienceRecord may write one SelfTag.\\\\n- One SelfTag points to zero or one predecessor but may support branch semantics.\\\\n- One VerificationReport belongs to one draft and one goal contract.\\\\n- One AgentComparisonRecord aggregates many normalized agent summaries.\\\\n\\\\n### Metadata requirements\\\\n\\\\nAll persisted entities should include:\\\\n\\\\n- timestamps\\\\n- provenance/source\\\\n- confidence class\\\\n- security classification\\\\n- scope (task-specific, user-specific, global)\\\\n- version ID\\\\n- retention rule\\\\n- whether the content is explicit, inferred, computed, or hypothetical\\\\n\\\\n### Versioning\\\\n\\\\n- Self-tags and valence maps must be explicitly versioned.\\\\n- Summary compaction must preserve references to source records.\\\\n- Schema evolution should be migration-safe.\\\\n\\\\n### Retention rules\\\\n\\\\n- Raw interactions may be retained only under approved policy.\\\\n- Sensitive data should support deletion, redaction, or summary-only retention.\\\\n- Derived valence maps should not require indefinite retention of raw sensitive data.\\\\n- Self-tags referencing removed content should preserve continuity through abstracted summary where policy permits.\\\\n\\\\n### Provenance and citation requirements\\\\n\\\\n- Every retrieved fact must preserve source identifiers.\\\\n- Every computed result must preserve command/query provenance.\\\\n- Every inferred statement must be labeled as inferred.\\\\n\\\\n## Workflow and Process Design\\\\n\\\\n### Canonical end-to-end reasoning
